<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精密装配在“最后毫米”区域需亚毫米级校正，但此时末端执行器和工件会遮挡视觉，导致视觉反馈失效。

Method: 提出ReTac-ACT模型，包含：(i) 双向交叉注意力实现视觉与触觉特征互增强；(ii) 本体感知条件门控网络，动态提升遮挡下的触觉权重；(iii) 触觉重建目标，聚焦学习操作相关接触信息而非通用纹理。

Result: 在NIST M1标准装配基准上达到90%插孔成功率，显著优于纯视觉及通用基线方法；在工业级0.1mm间隙下仍保持80%成功率；消融实验证明各模块均不可或缺。

Conclusion: ReTac-ACT有效融合视觉与触觉模态，解决了高精度装配中视觉遮挡下的控制难题，为接触密集型机器人操作提供了鲁棒、可泛化的解决方案。

Abstract: Precision assembly requires sub-millimeter corrections in contact-rich "last-millimeter" regions where visual feedback fails due to occlusion from the end-effector and workpiece. We present ReTac-ACT (Reconstruction-enhanced Tactile ACT), a vision-tactile imitation learning policy that addresses this challenge through three synergistic mechanisms: (i) bidirectional cross-attention enabling reciprocal visuo-tactile feature enhancement before fusion, (ii) a proprioception-conditioned gating network that dynamically elevates tactile reliance when visual occlusion occurs, and (iii) a tactile reconstruction objective enforcing learning of manipulation-relevant contact information rather than generic visual textures. Evaluated on the standardized NIST Assembly Task Board M1 benchmark, ReTac-ACT achieves 90% peg-in-hole success, substantially outperforming vision-only and generalist baseline methods, and maintains 80% success at industrial-grade 0.1mm clearance. Ablation studies validate that each architectural component is indispensable. The ReTac-ACT codebase and a vision-tactile demonstration dataset covering various clearance levels with both visual and tactile features will be released to support reproducible research.

### [390] [SCDP: Learning Humanoid Locomotion from Partial Observations via Mixed-Observation Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09574)
*Milo Carroll,Tianhu Peng,Lingfan Bao,Chengxu Zhou,Zhibin Li*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为传感器条件扩散策略（SCDP）的新方法，使类人机器人仅依靠机载传感器即可实现运动控制，无需复杂的全身状态估计。该方法通过混合观测训练、受限去噪、上下文分布对齐和上下文感知注意力掩码等技术，在部分可观测条件下隐式推断运动动力学，并在仿真与真实G1机器人上均取得优异性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有类人机器人运动控制方法依赖需要复杂且不可靠状态估计的特权全身状态，难以部署到实际机器人上。

Method: 提出传感器条件扩散策略（SCDP），采用混合观测训练（以传感器历史为条件、监督预测特权未来状态-动作轨迹），并引入受限去噪、上下文分布对齐和上下文感知注意力掩码来增强隐式状态估计并缓解训练-部署不匹配。

Result: 在仿真中，SCDP在速度指令控制任务中成功率99–100%，AMASS测试集运动跟踪成功率达93%，性能接近特权基线；在真实G1机器人上以50Hz成功部署，无需外部传感或显式状态估计。

Conclusion: SCDP有效实现了仅用机载传感器的高性能、可部署类人 locomotion 控制，显著降低了对可靠状态估计的依赖，推动了离线数据驱动策略向真实机器人落地的应用。

Abstract: Distilling humanoid locomotion control from offline datasets into deployable policies remains a challenge, as existing methods rely on privileged full-body states that require complex and often unreliable state estimation. We present Sensor-Conditioned Diffusion Policies (SCDP) that enables humanoid locomotion using only onboard sensors, eliminating the need for explicit state estimation. SCDP decouples sensing from supervision through mixed-observation training: diffusion model conditions on sensor histories while being supervised to predict privileged future state-action trajectories, enforcing the model to infer the motion dynamics under partial observability. We further develop restricted denoising, context distribution alignment, and context-aware attention masking to encourage implicit state estimation within the model and to prevent train-deploy mismatch. We validate SCDP on velocity-commanded locomotion and motion reference tracking tasks. In simulation, SCDP achieves near-perfect success on velocity control (99-100%) and 93% tracking success in AMASS test set, performing comparable to privileged baselines while using only onboard sensors. Finally, we deploy the trained policy on a real G1 humanoid at 50 Hz, demonstrating robust real robot locomotion without external sensing or state estimation.

Then, we integrate this estimation framework into a safety-critical control pipeline by formulating control barrier functions that provide rigorous safety guarantees. Experiments demonstrate that the proposed terrain estimation method provides smooth terrain representations. Moreover, the coupled estimation framework of terrain, state, and contact reduces the mean absolute error of base position estimation by 64.8%, decreases the estimation variance by 47.2%, and improves the robustness of contact estimation compared to a decoupled framework. *Haoyuan Li,Rui Liu,Hehe Fan,Yi Yang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出Step-Aware Contrastive Alignment (SACA)框架，通过感知驱动的步级审计与场景条件分组机制，从不完美轨迹中提取稠密监督信号，缓解VLN-CE任务中策略错误累积与稀疏奖励导致的梯度崩溃问题，显著提升泛化性、容错性与训练稳定性。

Abstract: Vision-Language Navigation in Continuous Environments (VLN-CE) requires agents to learn complex reasoning from long-horizon human interactions. While Multi-modal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have driven recent progress, current training paradigms struggle to balance generalization capability, error recovery and training stability. Specifically, (i) policies derived from SFT suffer from compounding errors, struggling to recover from out-of-distribution states, and (ii) Reinforcement Fine-Tuning (RFT) methods e.g. GRPO are bottlenecked by sparse outcome rewards. Their binary feedback fails to assign credit to individual steps, leading to gradient signal collapse in failure dominant batches. To address these challenges, we introduce Step-Aware Contrastive Alignment (SACA), a framework designed to extract dense supervision from imperfect trajectories. At its core, the Perception-Grounded Step-Aware auditor evaluates progress step-by-step, disentangling failed trajectories into valid prefixes and exact divergence points. Extensive experiments on VLN-CE benchmarks demonstrate that SACA achieves state-of-the-art performance.

Motivation: 解决现有视觉触觉传感器中不透明涂层阻碍预接触视觉、而透明涂层削弱触觉感知的固有矛盾。

Result: 在未见物体上验证了高泛化性与重建精度；在抓取任务中实现预接触视觉对齐与接触后触觉反馈的协同，显著提升感知能力。

Conclusion: MuxGel在不改变原有硬件结构前提下，成功拓展了视觉触觉传感器的多模态感知边界，兼具实用性与兼容性。

Abstract: High-fidelity visuo-tactile sensing is important for precise robotic manipulation. However, most vision-based tactile sensors face a fundamental trade-off: opaque coatings enable tactile sensing but block pre-contact vision. To address this, we propose MuxGel, a spatially multiplexed sensor that captures both external visual information and contact-induced tactile signals through a single camera. By using a checkerboard coating pattern, MuxGel interleaves tactile-sensitive regions with transparent windows for external vision. This design maintains standard form factors, allowing for plug-and-play integration into GelSight-style sensors by simply replacing the gel pad. To recover full-resolution vision and tactile signals from the multiplexed inputs, we develop a U-Net-based reconstruction framework. Leveraging a sim-to-real pipeline, our model effectively decouples and restores high-fidelity tactile and visual fields simultaneously. Experiments on unseen objects demonstrate the framework's generalization and accuracy. Furthermore, we demonstrate MuxGel's utility in grasping tasks, where dual-modality feedback facilitates both pre-contact alignment and post-contact interaction. Results show that MuxGel enhances the perceptual capabilities of existing vision-based tactile sensors while maintaining compatibility with their hardware stacks. Project webpage: https://zhixianhu.github.io/muxgel/.

</details>


### [398] [TIMID: Time-Dependent Mistake Detection in Videos of Robot Executions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09782)
*Nerea Gallego,Fernando Salanova,Claudio Mannarano,Cristian Mahulea,Eduardo Montijano*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为TIMID的新架构，用于检测机器人执行高层任务时的时间依赖性错误，通过视频和任务提示输入实现帧级错误预测，并支持弱监督训练与零样本仿真到现实迁移评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频异常检测（VAD）框架难以识别复杂的时间或空间任务违规，因其不表现为低层运动或动作错误；且缺乏针对机器人任务级时间错误的专用检测方法。

Method: 提出TIMID架构，融合视频与任务/错误提示作为输入，输出帧级错误存在预测；采用弱监督训练（每视频仅需一个标签）；构建含可控时间错误的多机器人仿真数据集，并支持零样本sim-to-real评估。

Result: 实验表明通用视觉语言模型（VLMs）缺乏显式时间推理能力，而TIMID能有效检测多种时间错误类型。

Conclusion: TIMID是一种专为机器人任务级时间错误检测设计的有效VAD-inspired框架，解决了现有方法在复杂任务异常识别上的不足，并验证了其在仿真与真实场景中的泛化能力。

Abstract: As robotic systems execute increasingly difficult task sequences, so does the number of ways in which they can fail. Video Anomaly Detection (VAD) frameworks typically focus on singular, low-level kinematic or action failures, struggling to identify more complex temporal or spatial task violations, because they do not necessarily manifest as low-level execution errors. To address this problem, the main contribution of this paper is a new VAD-inspired architecture, TIMID, which is able to detect robot time-dependent mistakes when executing high-level tasks. Our architecture receives as inputs a video and prompts of the task and the potential mistake, and returns a frame-level prediction in the video of whether the mistake is present or not. By adopting a VAD formulation, the model can be trained with weak supervision, requiring only a single label per video. Additionally, to alleviate the problem of data scarcity of incorrect executions, we introduce a multi-robot simulation dataset with controlled temporal errors and real executions for zero-shot sim-to-real evaluation. Our experiments demonstrate that out-of-the-box VLMs lack the explicit temporal reasoning required for this task, whereas our framework successfully detects different types of temporal errors. Project: https://ropertunizar.github.io/TIMID/

### [399] [Lightweight 3D LiDAR-Based UAV Tracking: An Adaptive Extended Kalman Filtering Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09783)
*Nivand Khosravi,Meysam Basiri,Rodrigo Ventura*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种轻量级、基于3D LiDAR的无人机相对定位跟踪系统，采用自适应扩展卡尔曼滤波（AEKF）框架，能有效处理稀疏、噪声大、非均匀的点云数据，并具备失效恢复能力，在GPS拒止环境下实现小无人机鲁棒、低功耗的相对定位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉跟踪易受光照影响，而传统LiDAR方案体积大、功耗高，不适用于小型无人机；亟需一种轻量、鲁棒、适用于弱信号与遮挡场景的LiDAR跟踪方法。

Method: 提出基于Livox Mid-360非重复扫描LiDAR的轻量跟踪系统，核心为自适应扩展卡尔曼滤波（AEKF）：利用新息与残差统计动态调整过程与观测噪声协方差矩阵，并设计检测失效时的跟踪恢复机制。

Result: 在DJI F550真实飞行实验中，该方法在稀疏点云和间歇检测下仍保持稳定跟踪，性能显著优于标准卡尔曼滤波与粒子滤波，尤其在剧烈机动时；可在无GPS、无需多传感器融合或外部基础设施条件下实现可靠相对定位。

Conclusion: 所提AEKF框架兼顾精度、鲁棒性与轻量化，为小型无人机在复杂环境下的自主协同与避障提供了可行的纯LiDAR相对定位解决方案。

Abstract: Accurate relative positioning is crucial for swarm aerial robotics, enabling coordinated flight and collision avoidance. Although vision-based tracking has been extensively studied, 3D LiDAR-based methods remain underutilized despite their robustness under varying lighting conditions. Existing systems often rely on bulky, power-intensive sensors, making them impractical for small UAVs with strict payload and energy constraints. This paper presents a lightweight LiDAR-based UAV tracking system incorporating an Adaptive Extended Kalman Filter (AEKF) framework. Our approach effectively addresses the challenges posed by sparse, noisy, and nonuniform point cloud data generated by non-repetitive scanning 3D LiDARs, ensuring reliable tracking while remaining suitable for small drones with strict payload constraints. Unlike conventional filtering techniques, the proposed method dynamically adjusts the noise covariance matrices using innovation and residual statistics, thereby enhancing tracking accuracy under real-world conditions. Additionally, a recovery mechanism ensures continuity of tracking during temporary detection failures caused by scattered LiDAR returns or occlusions. Experimental validation was performed using a Livox Mid-360 LiDAR mounted on a DJI F550 UAV in real-world flight scenarios. The proposed method demonstrated robust UAV tracking performance under sparse LiDAR returns and intermittent detections, consistently outperforming both standard Kalman filtering and particle filtering approaches during aggressive maneuvers. These results confirm that the framework enables reliable relative positioning in GPS-denied environments without the need for multi-sensor arrays or external infrastructure.

### [400] [Emerging Extrinsic Dexterity in Cluttered Scenes via Dynamics-aware Policy Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09882)
*Yixin Zheng,Jiangran Lyu,Yifan Zhang,Jiayi Chen,Mi Yan,Yuntian Deng,Xuesong Shi,Xiaoguang Zhao,Yizhou Wang,Zhizheng Zhang,He Wang*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种动态感知策略学习（DAPL）框架，通过显式建模杂乱环境中接触引发的物体动力学，提升非抓取式灵巧操作能力，无需手工设计接触启发式或复杂奖励工程，在仿真和真实世界中均取得显著性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法缺乏对杂乱场景中多物体间耦合接触动力学的显式建模，难以实现有效的非抓取式灵巧操作，限制了其在真实环境中的实用性。

Method: 提出Dynamics-Aware Policy Learning（DAPL）框架，结合显式世界建模学习接触诱导的动力学表征，并以此条件化强化学习策略训练。

Result: 在未见过的高密度杂乱仿真场景中成功率超基准方法25%以上；真实世界10个杂乱场景平均成功率约50%；在实际杂货分拣任务中验证了稳健的sim-to-real迁移能力。

Conclusion: DAPL通过数据驱动的动力学表征实现了无需人工先验的外源性灵巧操作，为复杂现实环境中的机器人操作提供了新范式。

Abstract: Extrinsic dexterity leverages environmental contact to overcome the limitations of prehensile manipulation. However, achieving such dexterity in cluttered scenes remains challenging and underexplored, as it requires selectively exploiting contact among multiple interacting objects with inherently coupled dynamics. Existing approaches lack explicit modeling of such complex dynamics and therefore fall short in non-prehensile manipulation in cluttered environments, which in turn limits their practical applicability in real-world environments. In this paper, we introduce a Dynamics-Aware Policy Learning (DAPL) framework that can facilitate policy learning with a learned representation of contact-induced object dynamics in cluttered environments. This representation is learned through explicit world modeling and used to condition reinforcement learning, enabling extrinsic dexterity to emerge without hand-crafted contact heuristics or complex reward shaping. We evaluate our approach in both simulation and the real world. Our method outperforms prehensile manipulation, human teleoperation, and prior representation-based policies by over 25% in success rate on unseen simulated cluttered scenes with varying densities. The real-world success rate reaches around 50% across 10 cluttered scenes, while a practical grocery deployment further demonstrates robust sim-to-real transfer and applicability.

### [401] [Robust Cooperative Localization in Featureless Environments: A Comparative Study of DCL, StCL, CCL, CI, and Standard-CL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09886)
*Nivand Khosravi,Meysam Basiri,Rodrigo Ventura*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文比较了五种协同定位（CL）方法在多机器人系统中的性能，发现StCL和Standard-CL精度最高但滤波不一致；DCL稳定性强；CI在一致性与精度间最平衡；CCL理论最优但对异常值敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为在GPS拒止环境下为多机器人系统选择合适的协同定位方法提供实践指导，需系统评估不同CL方法在精度、一致性与鲁棒性方面的权衡。

Method: 在ROS中实现五种CL方法（CCL、DCL、StCL、CI、Standard-CL），并通过蒙特卡洛仿真在弱数据关联和强检测两种条件下进行对比评估。

Result: StCL和Standard-CL位置误差最低但滤波严重不一致；DCL因测量步长机制表现出强稳定性；CI在一致性与精度间取得最佳平衡；CCL理论最优但易受测量异常值影响。

Conclusion: 不同CL方法存在本质权衡，应依据具体应用场景（如是否安全关键、对鲁棒性或精度的侧重）选择合适算法。

Abstract: Cooperative localization (CL) enables accurate position estimation in multi-robot systems operating in GPS-denied environments. This paper presents a comparative study of five CL approaches: Centralized Cooperative Localization (CCL), Decentralized Cooperative Localization (DCL), Sequential Cooperative Localization (StCL), Covariance Intersection (CI), and Standard Cooperative Localization (Standard-CL). All methods are implemented in ROS and evaluated through Monte Carlo simulations under two conditions: weak data association and robust detection. Our analysis reveals fundamental trade-offs among the methods. StCL and Standard-CL achieve the lowest position errors but exhibit severe filter inconsistency, making them unsuitable for safety-critical applications. DCL demonstrates remarkable stability under challenging conditions due to its measurement stride mechanism, which provides implicit regularization against outliers. CI emerges as the most balanced approach, achieving near-optimal consistency while maintaining competitive accuracy. CCL provides theoretically optimal estimation but shows sensitivity to measurement outliers. These findings offer practical guidance for selecting CL algorithms based on application requirements.

</details>


### [402] [NanoBench: A Multi-Task Benchmark Dataset for Nano-Quadrotor System Identification, Control, and State Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09908)
*Syed Izzat Ullah,Jose Baca*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文介绍了NanoBench，一个面向纳米级四旋翼（Crazyflie 2.1）的开源多任务基准数据集，提供高同步精度的底层传感器、执行器、控制器与估计器数据，支持非线性系统辨识、闭环控制评估和机载状态估计三大任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有空中机器人基准主要面向较大尺寸飞行器，缺乏纳米级四旋翼所需的执行器级信号；而纳米级平台受低雷诺数空气动力学、无芯直流电机非线性及算力限制影响，大尺度模型与控制器难以适用，亟需专用基准数据集。

Method: 构建基于Crazyflie 2.1（27g）在Vicon动捕环境下的NanoBench数据集，采集170+条涵盖悬停、激励、跟踪与激进机动的轨迹，同步记录Vicon真值、原始IMU、EKF估计、PID内部变量、PWM指令（100 Hz）及电池数据（10 Hz），并制定标准化评估协议与开源基线。

Result: 发布首个面向商用纳米级飞行器、同时提供执行器命令、控制器内部状态、估计器输出及毫米级真值的数据集；定义了三个任务的评估标准、训练/测试划分及开源基线模型。

Conclusion: NanoBench填补了纳米级空中机器人研究中高质量底层数据基准的空白，为开发适配低雷诺数、强非线性与资源受限特性的新模型与控制器提供了关键支撑。

Abstract: Existing aerial-robotics benchmarks target vehicles from hundreds of grams to several kilograms and typically expose only high-level state data. They omit the actuator-level signals required to study nano-scale quadrotors, where low-Reynolds number aerodynamics, coreless DC motor nonlinearities, and severe computational constraints invalidate models and controllers developed for larger vehicles. We introduce NanoBench, an open-source multi-task benchmark collected on the commercially available Crazyflie 2.1 nano-quadrotor (takeoff weight 27 g) in a Vicon motion capture arena. The dataset contains over 170 flight trajectories spanning hover, multi-frequency excitation, standard tracking, and aggressive maneuvers across multiple speed regimes. Each trajectory provides synchronized Vicon ground truth, raw IMU data, onboard extended Kalman filter estimates, PID controller internals, and motor PWM commands at 100 Hz, alongside battery telemetry at 10 Hz, aligned with sub-0.5 ms consistency. NanoBench defines standardized evaluation protocols, train/test splits, and open-source baselines for three tasks: nonlinear system identification, closed-loop controller benchmarking, and onboard state estimation assessment. To our knowledge, it is the first public dataset to jointly provide actuator commands, controller internals, and estimator outputs with millimeter-accurate ground truth on a commercially available nano-scale aerial platform.

### [403] [Kinodynamic Motion Retargeting for Humanoid Locomotion via Multi-Contact Whole-Body Trajectory Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09956)
*Xiaoyu Zhang,Steven Haener,Varun Madabushi,Maegan Tucker*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: KDMR是一种新型的人形机器人运动重定向框架，通过结合动力学约束和地面反作用力测量，解决了传统基于运动捕捉的重定向方法中存在的物理不一致性问题，显著提升了下游模仿学习策略的训练效率和运动稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于运动捕捉（MoCap）的重定向方法仅依赖空间数据，导致脚部滑动、地面穿透等物理不一致现象，严重影响下游模仿学习策略性能。

Method: 提出KinoDynamic Motion Retargeting（KDMR）框架，将重定向建模为多接触、全身轨迹优化问题；引入刚体动力学与接触互补性约束，并融合地面反作用力（GRF）测量以自动识别足部接触事件。

Result: 在动态可行性、GRF跟踪精度及下游控制策略训练效率与最终性能三方面均优于SOTA基线GMR；生成的动力学可行参考轨迹加速策略收敛并提升运动稳定性。

Conclusion: KDMR有效弥合了纯运动学重定向与真实物理交互之间的鸿沟，为高质量人形机器人运动生成与模仿学习提供了可靠基础；代码将在论文发表后开源。

Abstract: We present the KinoDynamic Motion Retargeting (KDMR) framework, a novel approach for humanoid locomotion that models the retargeting process as a multi-contact, whole-body trajectory optimization problem. Conventional kinematics-based retargeting methods rely solely on spatial motion capture (MoCap) data, inevitably introducing physically inconsistent artifacts, such as foot sliding and ground penetration, that severely degrade the performance of downstream imitation learning policies. To bridge this gap, KDMR extends beyond pure kinematics by explicitly enforcing rigid-body dynamics and contact complementarity constraints. Further, by integrating ground reaction force (GRF) measurements alongside MoCap data, our method automatically detects heel-toe contact events to accurately replicate complex human-like contact patterns. We evaluate KDMR against the state-of-the-art baseline, GMR, across three key dimensions: 1) the dynamic feasibility and smoothness of the retargeted motions, 2) the accuracy of GRF tracking compared to raw source data, and 3) the training efficiency and final performance of downstream control policies trained via the BeyondMimic framework. Experimental results demonstrate that KDMR significantly outperforms purely kinematic methods, yielding dynamically viable reference trajectories that accelerate policy convergence and enhance overall locomotion stability. Our end-to-end pipeline will be open-sourced upon publication.

</details>


### [404] [BEACON: Language-Conditioned Navigation Affordance Prediction under Occlusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09961)
*Xinyu Gao,Gang Chen,Javier Alonso-Mora*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出BEACON方法，通过在鸟瞰图（BEV）空间预测可通行区域热力图，解决语言条件局部导航中因遮挡导致目标定位困难的问题；其结合视觉语言模型与深度衍生的BEV特征，在遮挡场景下显著提升定位精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于视觉语言模型（VLM）的方法在图像空间进行2D预测，难以处理被家具或移动人体遮挡的区域，导致目标位置推理失败。

Method: BEACON将周围四向RGB-D观测和自然语言指令输入VLM，并注入空间线索；再将VLM输出与深度图生成的BEV特征融合，最终预测以自我为中心的BEV可通行性热力图。

Result: 在Habitat构建的遮挡感知数据集上，BEACON在验证集（含遮挡目标）上相较SOTA图像空间基线，按多种测地距离阈值平均准确率提升22.74个百分点。

Conclusion: 在BEV空间建模语言条件导航任务更鲁棒，尤其适用于存在动态/静态遮挡的真实场景；模块设计与BEV表征均被实验证实有效。

Abstract: Language-conditioned local navigation requires a robot to infer a nearby traversable target location from its current observation and an open-vocabulary, relational instruction. Existing vision-language spatial grounding methods usually rely on vision-language models (VLMs) to reason in image space, producing 2D predictions tied to visible pixels. As a result, they struggle to infer target locations in occluded regions, typically caused by furniture or moving humans. To address this issue, we propose BEACON, which predicts an ego-centric Bird's-Eye View (BEV) affordance heatmap over a bounded local region including occluded areas. Given an instruction and surround-view RGB-D observations from four directions around the robot, BEACON predicts the BEV heatmap by injecting spatial cues into a VLM and fusing the VLM's output with depth-derived BEV features. Using an occlusion-aware dataset built in the Habitat simulator, we conduct detailed experimental analysis to validate both our BEV space formulation and the design choices of each module. Our method improves the accuracy averaged across geodesic thresholds by 22.74 percentage points over the state-of-the-art image-space baseline on the validation subset with occluded target locations. Our project page is: https://xin-yu-gao.github.io/beacon.

</details>


### [405] [TiPToP: A Modular Open-Vocabulary Planning System for Robotic Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09971)
*William Shen,Nishanth Kumar,Sahit Chintalapudi,Jie Wang,Christopher Watson,Edward Hu,Jing Cao,Dinesh Jayaraman,Leslie Pack Kaelbling,Tomás Lozano-Pérez*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: TiPToP 是一个模块化系统，将预训练视觉基础模型与任务与运动规划器（TAMP）结合，直接从RGB图像和自然语言指令完成多步操作任务，无需任何机器人数据，在仿真与真实世界中均达到或超越需大量示范数据的VLA模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决现有端到端视觉语言动作（VLA）模型依赖大量特定机器人演示数据、泛化性差、可解释性低的问题，探索更简单、可扩展、可分析的模块化机器人操作范式。

Method: 构建TiPToP系统：将冻结的预训练视觉编码器（如ViT）与经典TAMP框架集成，利用视觉模型提取图像语义特征并映射至符号空间，由TAMP进行逻辑推理与运动规划；全程不微调视觉模型，零机器人数据训练。

Result: 在28个桌面操作任务（仿真+真实世界）上评估，TiPToP零样本性能匹配或优于需350小时演示数据微调的π₀.₅-DROID；173次试验的组件级失败分析揭示了视觉接地与符号映射等瓶颈；系统开源。

Conclusion: 模块化设计可在不牺牲性能前提下显著降低对机器人数据的依赖，提升可解释性与可调试性，为学习与规划融合提供新路径。

Abstract: We present TiPToP, an extensible modular system that combines pretrained vision foundation models with an existing Task and Motion Planner (TAMP) to solve multi-step manipulation tasks directly from input RGB images and natural-language instructions. Our system aims to be simple and easy-to-use: it can be installed and run on a standard DROID setup in under one hour and adapted to new embodiments with minimal effort. We evaluate TiPToP -- which requires zero robot data -- over 28 tabletop manipulation tasks in simulation and the real world and find it matches or outperforms $π_{0.5}\text{-DROID}$, a vision-language-action (VLA) model fine-tuned on 350 hours of embodiment-specific demonstrations. TiPToP's modular architecture enables us to analyze the system's failure modes at the component level. We analyze results from an evaluation of 173 trials and identify directions for improvement. We release TiPToP open-source to further research on modular manipulation systems and tighter integration between learning and planning. Project website and code: https://tiptop-robot.github.io

### [406] [Prompt-Driven Color Accessibility Evaluation in Diffusion-based Image Generation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09832)
*Xinyao Zhuang,Jose Echevarria,Kaan Akşit*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出CVDLoss新指标，用于评估生成图像对色觉障碍（CVD）用户的颜色可访问性，发现现有扩散模型难以可靠响应可访问性提示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 文本到图像生成在视觉质量和多样性上表现优异，但其对色觉障碍（CVD）用户颜色可访问性的支持尚未被系统研究。

Method: 采用现成的CVD模拟方法量化性能，并提出新指标CVDLoss，通过衡量图像梯度差异反映结构细节变化；验证其对达耳顿化（daltonization）等颜色可访问性处理的敏感性。

Result: CVDLoss被证实能有效检测颜色可访问性改进；实验表明当前预训练扩散模型无法稳定响应颜色可访问性提示。

Conclusion: CVDLoss是一种有价值的评估工具，可用于可访问性感知的图像生成与后处理，并揭示了当前生成模型在颜色可访问性方面的局限性。

Abstract: Generative models are increasingly integrated into creative workflows. While text-to-image generation excels in visual quality and diversity, color accessibility for users with Color Vision Deficiencies (CVD) remains largely unexplored. Our work systematically evaluates color accessibility in images generated by a common pretrained diffusion model, prompted to improve accessibility across diverse categories. We quantify performance using established, off-the-shelf CVD simulation methods and introduce "CVDLoss", a new metric measuring differences in image gradients indicative of structural detail. We validate CVDLoss against a commonly used daltonization method, demonstrating its sensitivity to color accessibility modifications. Applying CVDLoss to model outputs reveals that existing diffusion models struggle to reliably respond to accessibility-focused prompts. Consequently, our study establishes CVDLoss as a valuable evaluation tool for accessibility-aware image generation and post-processing, offering insights into current generative models' limitations in addressing color accessibility.

</details>


<div id='cs.MA'></div>

# cs.MA [[Back]](#toc)

### [407] [The Bureaucracy of Speed: Structural Equivalence Between Memory Consistency Models and Multi-Agent Authorization Revocation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09875)
*Vladyslav Parakhin*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种Capability Coherence System (CCS)，通过状态映射和Release Consistency-directed Coherence (RCC)策略，显著降低授权失效窗口内的未授权操作数，且安全边界与代理速度无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统身份与访问管理（IAM）在智能体执行场景下因时间假设失效而产生严重的授权一致性问题，尤其在高频率、低延迟的API调用中导致大量未授权操作。

Method: 定义Capability Coherence System（CCS），构建MESI状态到授权状态的结构保持映射φ，并在有界陈旧性语义下提出RCC策略；通过tick-based离散事件模拟，在三种业务场景中对比四种策略（含TTL租赁）的性能。

Result: RCC策略在高速场景下将未授权操作从6000降至50（120倍提升），异常触发撤销下提升184倍；所有120次仿真均无安全边界违反，验证了每能力级的安全保证。

Conclusion: RCC是一种与代理速度无关的新型访问控制一致性机制，从根本上摆脱了传统时间窗口策略的线性扩展缺陷，为高动态执行环境提供了严格可证的安全保障。

Abstract: The temporal assumptions underpinning conventional Identity and Access Management collapse under agentic execution regimes. A sixty-second revocation window permits on the order of $6 \times 10^3$ unauthorized API calls at 100 ops/tick; at AWS Lambda scale, the figure approaches $6 \times 10^5$. This is a coherence problem, not merely a latency problem. We define a Capability Coherence System (CCS) and construct a state-mapping $\varphi : Σ_{\rm MESI} \to Σ_{\rm auth}$ preserving transition structure under bounded-staleness semantics. A safety theorem bounds unauthorized operations for the execution-count Release Consistency-directed Coherence (RCC) strategy at $D_{\rm rcc} \leq n$, independent of agent velocity $v$ -- a qualitative departure from the $O(v \cdot \mathrm{TTL})$ scaling of time-bounded strategies. Tick-based discrete event simulation across three business-contextualised scenarios (four strategies, ten deterministic seeds each) confirms: RCC achieves a $120\times$ reduction versus TTL-based lease in the high-velocity scenario (50 vs. 6,000 unauthorized operations), and $184\times$ under anomaly-triggered revocation. Zero bound violations across all 120 runs confirm the per-capability safety guarantee. Simulation code: https://github.com/hipvlady/prizm

</details>


### [408] [Emotional Modulation in Swarm Decision Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09963)
*David Freire-Obregón*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文扩展了蜜蜂方程，构建了一个基于情感效价（正-负）和唤醒度（低-高）调节交互率的智能体模型，研究情感传染如何影响群体共识形成，并揭示情感不对称性与结构临界点共同塑造集体决策结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典群体决策理论（如蜜蜂方程）与情感建模结合，探究情绪如何通过调节招募与抑制过程影响共识动态。

Method: 在蜜蜂方程基础上构建情感调制的智能体模型，以效价-唤醒二维空间定义个体状态，并映射为模拟面部表情；通过三类情景分析情感对共识的影响。

Result: 情感调制可偏置决策结果并改变收敛速度；即使在情感对称条件下，系统内在非线性放大仍可导致决定性胜出； arousal可在valence相同时打破僵局，且存在支持阈值触发的‘雪球效应’。

Conclusion: 情感维度与结构临界点共同塑造集体决策，该框架为自然与人工系统中情感性集体选择提供了通用建模工具。

Abstract: Collective decision-making in biological and human groups often emerges from simple interaction rules that amplify minor differences into consensus. The bee equation, developed initially to describe nest-site selection in honeybee swarms, captures this dynamic through recruitment and inhibition processes. Here, we extend the bee equation into an agent-based model in which emotional valence (positive-negative) and arousal (low-high) act as modulators of interaction rates, effectively altering the recruitment and cross-inhibition parameters. Agents display simulated facial expressions mapped from their valence-arousal states, allowing the study of emotional contagion in consensus formation.
  Three scenarios are explored: (1) the joint effect of valence and arousal on consensus outcomes and speed, (2) the role of arousal in breaking ties when valence is matched, and (3) the "snowball effect" in which consensus accelerates after surpassing intermediate support thresholds. Results show that emotional modulation can bias decision outcomes and alter convergence times by shifting effective recruitment and inhibition rates. At the same time, intrinsic non-linear amplification can produce decisive wins even in fully symmetric emotional conditions.
  These findings link classical swarm decision theory with affective and social modelling, highlighting how both emotional asymmetries and structural tipping points shape collective outcomes. The proposed framework offers a flexible tool for studying the emotional dimensions of collective choice in both natural and artificial systems.

</details>
